NJORD Studio , Third-Party Software Licenses
============================================

NJORD Studio ships two programs: the studio app (njord-studio.exe) and the bundled
native 3D viewer (njord-viewer.exe). Both include the third-party open-source
components listed below, each used under its own license (reproduced in full).
These licenses govern only those components; NJORD Studio itself is proprietary
(see EULA.txt). (c) 2026 NJORD Studio AB.

#  NJORD Studio (app)
